### stemmimg
for word in data:
    token_words = word_tokenize(word)
    for i in token_words:
        stem_words = stemmer.stem(i)
        print(stem_words,end = ' ')

#### lemmatizing
for word in data:
    token_words = word_tokenize(word)
    for token in token_words:
        lemma_words = lem.lemmatize(token)
        print(lemma_words,end = ' ')

### name_entity_recognizing

for word in data:
    #print (data)
    named_entity = ne_chunk(pos_tag(word_tokenize(word)))
    print(named_entity)
    #f.write(named_entity)

### 3 -A ####
l = []
for word in data:
    token_words = word_tokenize(word)
    pos = pos_tag(token_words)
    #print(pos[0][0],j)
    for i, j in pos:
        if j=='PRP' or j=='PRP$':
            l.append((pos[0][0]))
            
            #print(pos[0][0],j)
            
### count of num of pronouns 
          
a = l
for i in set(a):
    x = l.count(i)
    print(i,x)
